</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:18pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International Reports Q2 Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:18pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>and Raises Full-Year Outlook </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net revenues declined 0.8% driven by unfavorable currency impacts; Organic Net Revenue<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> grew 4.6%, through a combination of volume/mix and pricing </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Diluted EPS was $0.55, up 162%, lapping prior-year impact from pension participation changes; Adjusted EPS<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> was $0.57, up 9% on a constant-currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

activities was $1.0&nbsp;billion; Free Cash Flow<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> was $581&nbsp;million </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Announcing 10% increase to quarterly dividend </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">DEERFIELD, Ill. &#150; July&nbsp;30, 2019 &#150; Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (NASDAQ: MDLZ) today reported its second quarter 2019
results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our strong second quarter performance demonstrates the potential of our strategy to accelerate volume-driven <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-line</FONT> growth in both developed and emerging markets,&#148; said Dirk Van de Put, Chairman and CEO. &#147;Our more consumer-centric mindset is driving investments in advertising and promotion of our global and
local brands, as well as accelerated innovation and improved distribution capabilities, building a sustainable foundation for long-term growth and value creation for our shareholders.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><U>Key Strategic Initiatives </U></I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company continued
to make good progress against the strategies of accelerating consumer-centric growth, driving operational excellence and building a winning growth culture this quarter. Examples included: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Expansion of Channels and Key Markets</B>:<B> </B>investing in fast-growing sales channels, including <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce,</FONT> and winning in high-potential emerging markets </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>

publication of the company&#146;s <I>Impact 2025</I> commitments, including its goals to source 100% of cocoa for its chocolate through Cocoa Life and achieve 100% packaging recyclability. In addition, the company reached an agreement with Enel
Green Power to source solar power in support of its goal to cut CO2 emissions in manufacturing by 15% by 2020. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><U>Second Quarter Commentary </U></I></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net revenues</B> declined 0.8&nbsp;percent, driven by the impact of currency. Organic Net Revenue increased
4.6&nbsp;percent, through a combination of volume/mix and pricing across both emerging and developed markets. There was a positive impact from lapping the Brazil trucking strike in the prior year. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross profit </B>declined $71&nbsp;million and margin decreased 90 basis points to 40.7&nbsp;percent due to
unfavorable year-over-year change in currency and commodity hedging activities. Adjusted Gross Profit<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> increased $106&nbsp;million at constant currency and margin was flat at 40.6&nbsp;percent.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating income </B>increased $544&nbsp;million and margin was 16.9&nbsp;percent, up 900 basis points, due to
lapping the prior-year impact from pension participation changes and lower Simplify to Grow Program costs. Adjusted Operating Income<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> increased by $41&nbsp;million at constant currency and margin
was flat at 16.7&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Diluted EPS</B> was $0.55, up 162&nbsp;percent, primarily due to lapping prior-year impact from pension
participation changes and prior-year loss on debt extinguishment and higher Adjusted EPS. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Adjusted EPS</B> was $0.57 and grew 9&nbsp;percent on a constant-currency basis, driven by earnings from
equity method investments, operating gains and share repurchases. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Capital Return</B>: The company returned approximately $700&nbsp;million to shareholders in common stock
repurchases and cash dividends. Year to date, the company has returned approximately $1.7&nbsp;billion. Today, the company&#146;s Board of Directors also declared a quarterly cash dividend of $0.285 per share of Class&nbsp;A common stock, an
increase of 10&nbsp;percent. This dividend is payable on October&nbsp;14, 2019, to shareholders recorded as of September&nbsp;30, 2019. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>2019 Outlook </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International
provides guidance on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis, as the company cannot predict some elements that are included in reported GAAP results, including the impact of foreign exchange. Refer to the Outlook section in the
discussion of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures below for more details. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">After strong first-half
performance, the company now expects Organic Net Revenue growth of 3+ percent. The company also increases its outlook for Adjusted EPS growth to ~5&nbsp;percent on a constant-currency basis. The company estimates currency translation would decrease
net revenue growth by approximately 3 percent<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP> with a negative $0.11 impact to Adjusted EPS<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>. In addition, the company continues to expect Free
Cash Flow of approximately $2.8&nbsp;billion. </P>
</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Conference Call </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International will host a conference call for investors with accompanying slides to review its results at 5 p.m. ET today. A
listen-only webcast will be provided at <U>www.mondelezinternational.com</U>. An archive of the webcast will be available on the company&#146;s web site. The company will be live tweeting the event at <U>www.twitter.com/MDLZ</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Mondel&#275;z International </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (NASDAQ: MDLZ) empowers people to snack right in over 150 countries around the world. With 2018 net revenues
of approximately $26&nbsp;billion, MDLZ is leading the future of snacking with iconic global and local brands such as <I>Oreo</I>, <I>belVita</I> and <I>LU</I> biscuits; <I>Cadbury Dairy Milk</I>, <I>Milka</I> and <I>Toblerone</I> chocolate; <I>Sour
Patch Kids</I> candy and <I>Trident</I> gum. Mondel&#275;z International is a proud member of the Standard and Poor&#146;s 500, Nasdaq 100 and Dow Jones Sustainability Index. Visit <U>www.mondelezinternational.com</U> or follow the company on
Twitter at <U>www.twitter.com/MDLZ</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>End Notes </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Additional Definitions </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Emerging markets
consist of the Latin America region in its entirety; the Asia, Middle East and Africa region excluding Australia, New Zealand and Japan; and the following countries from the Europe region: Russia, Ukraine, Turkey, Kazakhstan, Belarus, Georgia,
Poland, Czech Republic, Slovak Republic, Hungary, Bulgaria, Romania, the Baltics and the East Adriatic countries. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Developed markets
include the entire North America region, the Europe region excluding the countries included in the emerging markets definition, and Australia, New Zealand and Japan from the Asia, Middle East and Africa region. </P>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><U>Schedule 3 </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. and Subsidiaries </B></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. and Subsidiaries </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Reconciliation of GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>(Unaudited) </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company reports its
financial results in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States (&#147;GAAP&#148;). However, management believes that also presenting certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures
provides additional information to facilitate the comparison of the company&#146;s historical operating results and trends in its underlying operating results, and provides additional transparency on how the company evaluates its business.
Management uses these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in making financial, operating and planning decisions and in evaluating the company&#146;s performance. The company also believes that presenting these
measures allows investors to view its performance using the same measures that the company uses in evaluating its financial and business performance and trends. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company considers quantitative and qualitative factors in assessing whether to adjust for the impact of items that may be significant or that could affect
an understanding of its ongoing financial and business performance and trends. The adjustments generally fall within the following categories: acquisition&nbsp;&amp; divestiture activities, gains and losses on intangible asset sales and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairments, major program restructuring activities, constant currency and related adjustments, major program financing and hedging activities and other major items affecting comparability of operating
results. See below for a description of adjustments to the company&#146;s U.S. GAAP financial measures included herein. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> information should be considered as supplemental in nature and is not meant to be considered in isolation or
as a substitute for the related financial information prepared in accordance with U.S. GAAP. In addition, the company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures may not be the same as or comparable to similar <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures presented by other companies. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Because GAAP financial measures on a forward-looking basis are not
accessible and reconciling information is not available without unreasonable effort, the company has not provided that information with regard to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the company&#146;s outlook.
Refer to the Outlook section below for more details. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>DEFINITIONS OF THE COMPANY&#146;S <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL
MEASURES </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures and corresponding metrics reflect how the company
evaluates its operating results currently and provide improved comparability of operating results. As new events or circumstances arise, these definitions could change. When these definitions change, the company provides the updated definitions and
presents the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> historical results on a comparable basis. When items no longer impact the company&#146;s current or future presentation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
operating results, the company removes these items from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> definitions. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>&#147;Organic Net Revenue&#148;</B> is defined as net revenues excluding the impacts of acquisitions,
divestitures and currency rate fluctuations. The company also evaluates Organic Net Revenue growth from emerging and developed markets. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>&#147;Adjusted Gross Profit&#148;</B> is defined as gross profit excluding the impacts of the Simplify to Grow
Program; acquisition integration costs; the operating results of divestitures; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts from commodity and forecasted currency transaction derivative
contracts; and incremental expenses related to the 2017 malware incident. The company also presents &#147;Adjusted Gross Profit margin,&#148; which is subject to the same adjustments as Adjusted Gross Profit. The company also evaluates growth in the
company&#146;s Adjusted Gross Profit on a constant currency basis. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>&#147;Adjusted Operating Income&#148;</B> and <B>&#147;Adjusted Segment Operating Income&#148;</B> are defined
as operating income (or segment operating income) excluding the impacts of the items listed in the Adjusted Gross Profit definition as well as gains or losses (including <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges) on
goodwill and intangible assets; divestiture or acquisition gains or losses and related divestiture, acquisition and integration costs; remeasurement of net monetary position; impacts from resolution of tax matters; CEO transition remuneration; and
impact from pension participation changes. The company also presents &#147;Adjusted Operating Income margin&#148; and &#147;Adjusted Segment Operating Income margin&#148;, which are subject to the same adjustments as Adjusted Operating Income and
Adjusted Segment Operating Income. The company also evaluates growth in the company&#146;s Adjusted Operating Income and Adjusted Segment Operating Income on a constant currency basis. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>&#147;Adjusted EPS&#148;</B> is defined as diluted EPS attributable to Mondel&#275;z International from
continuing operations excluding the impacts of the items listed in the Adjusted Operating Income definition, as well as losses on debt extinguishment and related expenses; gains or losses on equity method investment transactions; net earnings from
divestitures; gains or losses on interest rate swaps no longer designated as accounting cash flow hedges due to changed financing and hedging plans; and U.S. tax reform discrete impacts. Similarly, within Adjusted EPS, the company&#146;s equity
method investment net earnings exclude its proportionate share of its investees&#146; unusual or infrequent items. The tax impact of each of the items excluded from the company&#146;s GAAP results was computed based on the facts and tax assumptions
associated with each item, and such impacts have also been excluded from Adjusted EPS. The company also evaluates growth in the company&#146;s Adjusted EPS on a constant currency basis. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

expenditures. Free Cash Flow is the company&#146;s primary measure used to monitor its cash flow performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">See the attached

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>SEGMENT OPERATING INCOME </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company uses segment operating income to evaluate segment performance and allocate resources. The company believes it is appropriate to disclose this
measure to help investors analyze segment performance and trends. Segment operating income excludes unrealized gains and losses on hedging activities (which are a component of cost of sales), general corporate expenses (which are a component of
selling, general and administrative expenses), amortization of intangibles, gains and losses on divestitures and acquisition-related costs (which are a component of selling, general and administrative expenses) in all periods presented. The company
excludes these items from segment operating income in order to provide better transparency of its segment operating results. Furthermore, the company centrally manages benefit plan <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income and
interest and other expense, net. Accordingly, the company does not present these items by segment because they are excluded from the segment profitability measure that management reviews. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>ITEMS IMPACTING COMPARABILITY OF OPERATING RESULTS </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
following information is provided to give qualitative and quantitative information related to items impacting comparability of operating results. The company identifies these based on how management views the company&#146;s business; makes
financial, operating and planning decisions; and evaluates the company&#146;s ongoing performance. In addition, the company discloses the impact of changes in currency exchange rates on the company&#146;s financial results in order to reflect
results on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Divestitures, Divestiture-related costs and Gains/(losses) on Divestitures </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Divestitures include completed sales of businesses and exits of major product lines upon completion of a sale or licensing agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">On May&nbsp;28, 2019, the company completed the sale of most of its cheese business in the Middle East and Africa
to Arla Foods of Denmark. The company recorded a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $41&nbsp;million on the sale. The company also incurred divestiture-related costs of $11&nbsp;million in the three months and $10&nbsp;million
in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2019. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">On April&nbsp;28, 2017, the company completed the sale of several manufacturing facilities in France and the sale
or license of several local confectionery brands. During the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018, the company reversed $3&nbsp;million of accrued expenses no longer required. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Acquisitions, Acquisition-related costs and Acquisition integration costs </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On June&nbsp;19, 2019, the company announced an agreement to acquire a majority interest in Perfect Snacks, a pioneer in the fast-growing refrigerated
nutrition bars segment. The company completed this transaction on July&nbsp;16, 2019. In connection with this transaction, the company incurred acquisition-related costs of $1&nbsp;million in the three months and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2019.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On June&nbsp;7, 2018, the company acquired a U.S. premium biscuit company, Tate&#146;s Bake Shop, within its North America segment and extended its
premium biscuit offerings. On a constant currency basis, the purchase added incremental net revenues of $15&nbsp;million in the three months and $35&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2019. In addition, the company incurred
acquisition-related costs of $13&nbsp;million in the three months and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Within the company&#146;s AMEA segment, in
connection with the acquisition of a biscuit operation in Vietnam in 2015, the company recorded integration costs of $2&nbsp;million in the three months and $3&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Simplify to Grow Program </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On September&nbsp;6, 2018, the company&#146;s Board of Directors approved an extension of the restructuring program through 2022, an increase of
$1.3&nbsp;billion in the program charges and an increase of $700&nbsp;million in capital expenditures. The current restructuring program, as increased and extended by these actions, is now called the Simplify to Grow Program. The primary objective
of the Simplify to Grow Program is to reduce the company&#146;s operating cost structure in both its supply chain and overhead costs. The program covers severance as well as asset disposals and other manufacturing and procurement-related <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> costs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Restructuring costs </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company recorded restructuring charges of $20&nbsp;million in the three months and $40&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2019 and
$112&nbsp;million in the three months and $164&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018 within asset impairment and exit costs and benefit plan <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income. These charges were for <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> asset write-downs (including accelerated depreciation and asset impairments), severance and other related costs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Implementation costs </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Implementation costs primarily
relate to reorganizing the company&#146;s operations and facilities in connection with its supply chain reinvention program and other identified productivity and cost saving initiatives. The costs include incremental expenses related to the closure
of facilities, costs to terminate certain contracts and the simplification of the company&#146;s information systems. The company recorded implementation costs of $68&nbsp;million in the three months and $118&nbsp;million in the six months ended
June&nbsp;30, 2019 and $70&nbsp;million in the three months and $132&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts from commodity and currency derivative contracts </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company excludes unrealized gains and losses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts) from
outstanding commodity and forecasted currency transaction derivatives from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> earnings measures until such time that the related exposures impact its operating results. The company recorded net
unrealized gains on commodity and forecasted currency transaction derivatives of $33&nbsp;million in the three months and $49&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2019 and $88&nbsp;million in the three months and $294&nbsp;million in
the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Remeasurement of net monetary position </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the second quarter of 2018, primarily based on published estimates which indicated that Argentina&#146;s three-year cumulative inflation rate exceeded
100%, the company concluded that Argentina became a highly inflationary economy for accounting purposes. As of July&nbsp;1, 2018, the company began to apply highly inflationary accounting for its Argentinian subsidiaries and changed their functional
currency from the Argentinian peso to the U.S. dollar. On July&nbsp;1, 2018, both monetary and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-monetary</FONT> assets and liabilities denominated in Argentinian pesos were remeasured into U.S. dollars. As of each
subsequent balance sheet date, Argentinian peso denominated monetary assets and liabilities were remeasured into U.S. dollars using the exchange rate as of the balance sheet date, with remeasurement and other transaction gains and losses recorded in
net earnings. The company recorded a $1&nbsp;million remeasurement gain in the three months and a $1&nbsp;million dollar loss in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2019, within selling, general and administrative expenses related to the valuation of
the Argentinian peso denominated net monetary assets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Impact from pension participation changes </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The impact from pension participation changes represent the charges incurred when employee groups are withdrawn from multiemployer pension plans and other
changes in employee group pension plan participation. The company excludes these charges from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> results because those amounts do not reflect the company&#146;s ongoing pension obligations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During 2018, the company executed a complete withdrawal from the Bakery and Confectionery Union and Industry International Pension Fund (&#147;Fund&#148;) and
recorded an estimate of the withdrawal liability. On July&nbsp;11, 2019, the company received a withdrawal liability assessment from the Fund totaling $526&nbsp;million and requiring <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pro-rata</FONT> monthly payments
over 20 years. To meet this obligation, the company will begin payments during the </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
second half of 2019. Within selling, general and administrative expenses, the company recorded a $35&nbsp;million ($26&nbsp;million net of tax) adjustment in the three months ended June&nbsp;30,
2019 and a $408&nbsp;million ($305&nbsp;million net of tax) estimated charge in the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018, related to the discounted withdrawal liability. As of June&nbsp;30, 2019, the discounted withdrawal liability was
$396&nbsp;million, with $22&nbsp;million recorded in other current liabilities and $374&nbsp;million recorded in long-term other liabilities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Impact from resolution of tax matters </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A tax
indemnification matter related to the company&#146;s 2007 acquisition of the LU biscuit business was closed during the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018. The closure had no impact on net earnings; however, it did result in a $15&nbsp;million tax
benefit that was fully offset by an $11&nbsp;million expense in selling, general and administrative expenses and a $4&nbsp;million expense in interest and other expense, net. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>CEO transition remuneration </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On November&nbsp;20,
2017, Dirk Van de Put succeeded Irene Rosenfeld as CEO of Mondel&#275;z International. In order to incent Mr.&nbsp;Van de Put to join the company, the company provided him compensation to make him whole for incentive awards he forfeited or grants
that were not made to him when he left his former employer. In connection with Irene Rosenfeld&#146;s retirement, the company made her outstanding grants of performance share units for the 2016-2018 and 2017-2019 performance cycles eligible for
continued vesting and paid $0.5&nbsp;million salary for her service as Chairman from January through March 2018. The company refers to these elements of Mr.&nbsp;Van de Put&#146;s and Ms.&nbsp;Rosenfeld&#146;s compensation arrangements together as
&#147;CEO transition remuneration.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company is excluding amounts it expenses as CEO transition remuneration from its <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> results because those amounts are not part of the company&#146;s regular compensation program and are incremental to amounts the company would have incurred as ongoing CEO compensation. The company incurred
CEO transition remuneration of $3&nbsp;million in the three months and $6&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2019 and $10&nbsp;million in the three months and $14&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Gain related to interest rate swaps </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company
recognized a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> loss of $5&nbsp;million in the three months and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $9&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018, within interest and
other expense, net related to certain forward-starting interest rate swaps for which the planned timing of the related forecasted debt was changed. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Loss on debt extinguishment </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On April&nbsp;17,
2018, the company completed a cash tender offer and retired $570&nbsp;million of long-term U.S. dollar debt. The company recorded a loss on debt extinguishment of $140&nbsp;million within interest and other expense, net related to the amount the
company paid to retire the debt in excess of its carrying value and from recognizing unamortized discounts, deferred financing and other cash costs in earnings at the time of the debt extinguishment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>U.S. tax reform discrete impacts </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On
December&nbsp;22, 2017, the United States enacted tax reform legislation that included a broad range of business tax provisions, including but not limited to a reduction in the U.S. federal tax rate from 35% to 21%, as well as provisions that limit
or eliminate various deductions or credits. The legislation also causes U.S. allocated expenses (e.g. interest and general administrative expense) to be taxed and imposes a new tax on U.S. cross-border payments. Furthermore, the legislation includes
a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> transition tax on accumulated foreign earnings and profits. While clarifying guidance was issued by the Internal Revenue Service (&#147;IRS&#148;) during 2018, further tax legislative guidance is
expected during 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018, the company recorded $87&nbsp;million in discrete net tax costs primarily comprised
of an increase to its transition tax liability of $86&nbsp;million as a result of additional guidance issued by the IRS and various state taxing authorities, new state legislation enacted during the period and further refinement of various
components of the underlying calculations. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Gains and losses on equity method investment transactions </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As of June&nbsp;30, 2019, the company held a 13.6% ownership interest in KDP. The company&#146;s ownership interest in KDP may change over time due to
stock-based compensation arrangements and other transactions by KDP. During the first quarter of 2019, the company recognized a $23&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain related to the impact of a KDP acquisition that
decreased the company&#146;s ownership interest from 13.8% to 13.6%. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On March&nbsp;7, 2016, the company exchanged a portion of its 43.5% JDE equity
interest for a new equity interest in Keurig Green Mountain, Inc. (&#147;Keurig&#148;). Following the transaction, the company&#146;s JDE equity interest became 26.5% and the company&#146;s new Keurig equity interest was 24.2%. During the first
quarter of 2016, the company recorded the difference between the $2&nbsp;billion fair value of Keurig and the company&#146;s basis in the exchanged JDE shares as a gain of $43&nbsp;million. In the second quarter of 2019, the company determined that
an adjustment to accumulated other comprehensive losses related to its JDE investment was required, which reduced the company&#146;s previously reported gain by $29&nbsp;million. The company recorded the adjustment in the net loss on equity method
transactions in the second quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the second quarter of 2019, the company also recorded an additional
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $4&nbsp;million related to the 2018 sale of one of its equity method investments. This additional gain relates to the release of funds previously held in escrow. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Equity method investee adjustments </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Within
Adjusted EPS, the company&#146;s equity method investment net earnings exclude its proportionate share of its investees&#146; unusual or infrequent items, such as acquisition and divestiture-related costs, restructuring program costs and discrete
U.S. tax reform impacts recorded by the company&#146;s JDE and KDP equity method investees. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Constant currency </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management evaluates the operating performance of the company and its international subsidiaries on a constant currency basis. The company determines its
constant currency operating results by dividing or multiplying, as appropriate, the current period local currency operating results by the currency exchange rates used to translate the company&#146;s financial statements in the comparable prior-year
period to determine what the current-period U.S. dollar operating results would have been if the currency exchange rate had not changed from the comparable prior-year period. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>OUTLOOK </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company&#146;s outlook for 2019 Organic Net Revenue growth, Adjusted EPS growth on a constant currency basis and Free Cash Flow are <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures that exclude or otherwise adjust for items impacting comparability of financial results such as the impact of changes in currency exchange rates, restructuring activities, acquisitions
and divestitures. The company is not able to reconcile its projected Organic Net Revenue growth to its projected reported net revenue growth for the full-year 2019 because the company is unable to predict during this period the impact from potential
acquisitions or divestitures, as well as the impact of currency translation due to the unpredictability of future changes in currency exchange rates, which could be material as a significant portion of the company&#146;s operations are outside the
U.S. The company is not able to reconcile its projected Adjusted EPS growth on a constant currency basis to its projected reported diluted EPS growth for the full-year 2019 because the company is unable to predict during this period the timing of
its restructuring program costs, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts from commodity and forecasted currency transaction derivative contracts and impacts from potential acquisitions
or divestitures well as the impact of currency translation due to the unpredictability of future changes in currency exchange rates, which could be material as a significant portion of the company&#146;s operations are outside the U.S. The company
is not able to reconcile its projected Free Cash Flow to its projected net cash from operating activities for the full-year 2019 because the company is unable to predict during this period the timing and amount of capital expenditures impacting cash
flow. Therefore, because of the uncertainty and variability of the nature and amount of future adjustments, which could be significant, the company is unable to provide a reconciliation of these measures without unreasonable effort. </P>
</DIV></Center>

<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. and Subsidiaries </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Reconciliation of GAAP to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures </B></P>
